crying wojak, also called frustrated wojak or, more rarely, angry wojak or it's not fair wojak, is a variation on the wojak face, driven to tears and clenching his teeth. it was used by internet users to express sadness and frustration, on their own behalf or speaking about other people, and has been an inspiration for many other wojak memes.
